<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ото-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oto-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оторвать.html>оторва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otorvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрывать.html>отрыва́ть</a></b>)

***оторваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оторваться.html>оторва́ться</a> (3457)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оторвать.html>оторва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оторваться.html>оторва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otorvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрываться.html>отрыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to come off; to tear off; to be torn off</li>
<li>(of an aircraft) to take off</li>
<li>to turn away, to tear oneself away (from work, a book. etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отрываться.html>отрыва́ясь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>otryvájasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">without stopping work; without rest; nonstop</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to separate, to disengage (from pursuit)</li>
<li>to lose contact (with someone)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have a break, to rest from daily routine</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оторвать.html>оторва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рва́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6°b/c".     <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>Фо́рма</a> ед. ч. м. р. прош. вр. <i>«<a href = vnd.unilang:оторваться.html>оторвался́</a>»</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:являться.html>явля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вшей</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:отрываться.html>отрыва́ться</a>.

***оторопеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оторопеть.html>оторопе́ть</a> (9596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оторопь.html>о́торопь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ótoropʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпадать.html>отпада́ть</a> (14344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отпад-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otpad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпадать.html>отпада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпасть.html>отпа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall off, to fall away</li>
<li>to break away <i>(from)</i></li>
<li>to be dismissed, to fall away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпадать.html>отпада́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">voprós <b>otpadájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the question stands no longer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(wish, desire)</i> to pass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">и́з-за <a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>ды́ма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпадать.html>отпада́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:желание.html>жела́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">íz-za dýma u menjá <b>otpadájet</b> želánije jestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the smoke puts me off eating</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:падать.html>па́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pádatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпадать.html>отпа́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpádatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to stop falling</li></ol>

***отпасть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпасть.html>отпа́сть</a> (11708)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпасть.html>отпа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпадать.html>отпада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall off, to fall away</li>
<li>to break away <i>(from)</i></li>
<li>to be dismissed, to fall away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ния</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпасть.html>отпа́ли</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vse somnénija <b>otpáli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">all doubt fell away</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идея.html>иде́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпасть.html>отпа́ла</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éta idéja <b>otpála</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">that idea was dismissed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(wish, desire)</i> to pass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">и́з-за <a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>ды́ма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпадать.html>отпада́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:желание.html>жела́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">íz-za dýma u menjá <b>otpadájet</b> želánije jestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the smoke puts me off eating</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпасть.html>отпа́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тому</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>otpála</b> oxóta k étomu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his desire to do it has passed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become redundant, to fall out of use</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпеваемый.html>отпева́емый</a> (32215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпеваемый.html>отпева́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpevájemyj</span>)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пе́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тый</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>от-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-пе-</b>; суффикс: <b>-т</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпечатать.html>отпеча́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpečátatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отпеча́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to print, to type
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпечатать.html>отпеча́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тираж.html>тира́ж</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpečátatʹ</b> vesʹ tiráž knígi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to print the whole edition of the book</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to imprint</li>
<li>to unseal, to open up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say brusquely/resolutely/emphatically
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">"<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойду́</a>", - <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпечатать.html>отпеча́тала</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">"ne pojdú", - <b>otpečátala</b> oná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">"I will not go," she said with emphasis</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***отпечататься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпечататься.html>отпеча́таться</a> (22612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпечатать.html>отпеча́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otpečátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпечататься.html>отпеча́таться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpečátatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отпеча́тываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be imprinted, to leave tracks <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of one's feet in the snow</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be imprinted, to remain indelibly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the mind, soul, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to manifest outwardly, to become evident, to be visible
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочарование.html>разочарова́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпечататься.html>отпеча́талось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лице́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razočarovánije <b>otpečátalosʹ</b> na jevó licé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">disappointment was stamped (<b>became evident</b>) on his face</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпечатать.html>отпеча́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otpečátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пи.html>пи</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>ра́ть</a></b>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпирать.html>отпира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otpirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
